# Weights Archive Index ‚ÄĒ Tay/Ho/joo_kai .h5 RL agents
**Source of truth for these weights is the external archive at `../mtdsim-weights-archive/` (sibling of this repo), NOT git.** All listed blobs are absent from the current `HEAD` working tree; they survive in git only via historical commits on side branches. A future history rewrite (e.g. `git filter-repo --strip-blobs-bigger-than`, BFG, or aggressive `git gc --prune=now` after the side branches are deleted) can drop them permanently. The external archive is what guarantees recovery.
## Recovery procedure (if the archive is lost but the git object store survives)
Each row records the blob SHA. As long as the object is still in the local repo's `.git/objects/` (or any clone with the relevant branches), recovery is:
```bash
git cat-file -p <blob_sha> > <restored_name>.h5
# verify integrity
sha256sum <restored_name>.h5   # must match the sha256 column
```
Confirm the blob is still retrievable with `git cat-file -e <blob_sha>` before relying on this.
## Summary
- **Total distinct `.h5` blobs found across all history & all refs:** 198
- **`history-only` (absent from current HEAD tree):** 198
- **`present-in-tree` (still on disk at current HEAD):** 0
- **Extracted to external archive:** 198 files, 116.0 MiB total
- **Archive path:** `/home/marc/GitHub/mtdsim-weights-archive/`
- **Checksums file:** `mtdsim-weights-archive/CHECKSUMS.sha256` (sha256 of every extracted file)
- **All 198 blobs verified retrievable** via `git cat-file -e <sha>`; sha256 of every extracted file matches the value recorded in this index.
- **Branch-tip reachability:** 181 blobs are referenced from at least one branch tip tree (still kept alive by that ref); 17 blobs are reachable only from historical commits (more exposed to GC if those commits become unreachable).

## Scope and method
- Enumerated via `git rev-list --all --objects | grep '\.h5$'` (198 unique blob SHAs).
- Introduction & deletion commits parsed from `git log --all -m --raw --reverse -- '*.h5'`. `-m` is required to surface blobs first introduced via a merge.
- `path` is the canonical path as listed by `rev-list`. Renames preserve the same blob SHA; the introducing commit may be at an earlier (different) path.
- `provisional_label` is inferred **from the filename alone** ‚ÄĒ **UNVERIFIED**. It is NOT a mapping to any published ablation / config / experiment. That reconciliation is deferred eval/ablation work.
- `siblings` shows other files touched in the introducing and deleting commits, capped at 6 most-relevant (`.h5` first, then config/code/data); large bulk-import commits are summarised with `+N more`.
